		<div id = "mainArea" class = "mainArea"> 

                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         <div class="FirstEle">      <p>      <strong>Stock market today: </strong>On account of the sharp sell-off in PSU stocks, the Indian <a class="manualbacklink" target="_blank" href="https://www.livemint.com/market">stock market</a> gave up early morning gains and ended lower on Monday. The Nifty 50 index lost 166 points and closed at the 21,616 level, the <a class="autobacklink-topic" target="_blank" href="https://www.livemint.com/market/market-stats/stocks-bse-share-price-nse-bse-S0004751" data-name="BSE">BSE</a> Sensex nosedived 523 points and finished at the 71,072 mark while the Bank Nifty index crashed 752 points and ended at the 44,882 level. In the broad market, the small-cap index crashed 3.16 percent whereas the mid-cap index tanked 2.62 percent.</p>   </div>   
<div id="aniview-ads">
	<div id="adHeightstory" class="adHeight280"> 
		<div class="adHolderStory storyadHolderAfterLoad" id="story-ads-0"> 
		<script> googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('story-ads-0'); }); </script> 
		</div>
	</div>
</div> 
               <div class="paywall" id="paywall_11707789480363">        <p>   "Domestic equities opened positive but soon witnessed selling pressure amid muted global cues. While Nifty closed with a loss of 166 points (-0.8%) at 21616, the broader market plunged sharply with the Nifty mid-cap 100 down 2.5% and the Nifty small-cap 100 down 4%. The volatility index - India VIX jumped 4% to 16 levels. Barring IT &amp; Pharma, all sectors ended in red. PSUs saw a heavy profit booking after witnessing a sharp rally over the last few months and weak Q3 results posted by many. There was also caution ahead of domestic CPI and IIP data that is due for release later on Monday," said Siddhartha Khemka, Head - Retail Research at Motilal Oswal.</p>        				<div class="trendingSimilarHeight">
		<div class="moreNews  widget-impression-candidate lmWidgetTracking" data-vars-widget-type="storyWidget" data-vars-widget-name = "Trending Inline Widget" data-vars-widget-title = "Trending Stories" data-vars-orderid="1" id = "tr_11707789480363" style = "display:none;" data-vars-ab="trending" data-vars-pos="trending"  data-vars-class="trending" data-vars-widgettype = "trending" data-vars-widgetId= "0002">
		</div>
		</div>
	
              <p>   <strong>Also Read:</strong> <a class="manualbacklink" target="_blank" href="https://www.livemint.com/market/stock-market-news/stock-market-today-ashok-leyland-bandhan-bank-pnb-zeel-among-13-stocks-under-f-o-ban-list-today-11707744514066.html">Ashok Leyland, Bandhan Bank, PNB, ZEEL, among 13 stocks under F&amp;O ban list today</a></p>     <div class="subscribeAd" id="subscribeAd"> <div id="subscribed-11707789480363"></div> <script> if (adFreesubs || adLite) { getGooglePubAds("subs-adfree"); }</script> </div>                   <p>   <h2>Day trading guide for stock market today</h2><p>On the outlook for the Nifty 50 index, Nagaraj Shetti, Senior Technical Research Analyst at HDFC Securities said, "A long bear candle was formed on the daily chart that placed it at the edge of the downside breakout of the crucial support of up trend line at 21,600 levels. The weakness in the benchmark Nifty was accompanied by a deep cut in the broader market indices like midcap and small-cap segments on Monday. This is not a good sign. The short-term trend of Nifty is negative. The benchmark and broader market indices are now placed to show further weakness in the near term. The next lower support for the Nifty is at 21,200 to 21,150 levels for this week. Immediate resistance for Nifty today is placed at 21,800 levels."</p>                      <p>   On the outlook for the Bank Nifty today, Om Mehra, Technical Analyst at SAMCO Securities said, "In the realm of Bank Nifty, the session concluded at 44,882.25, witnessing a loss of 752 points or 1.65 percent. PSU banks bore the brunt, experiencing a significant 4.66% decline. None of the Nifty Bank constituent closed in the green signifying intense selling across the sector. function isGaa() {
  // Validate GAA params.
  const params = getQueryParams();
  if (!params.gaa_at) {
    return false;
  }
  if (!params.gaa_n) {
    console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_n` URL param is missing.');
    return false;
  }
  if (!params.gaa_sig) {
    console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_sig` URL param is missing.');
    return false;
  }
  if (!params.gaa_ts) {
    console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_ts` URL param is missing.');
    return false;
  }
  if (parseInt(params.gaa_ts, 16) < Date.now() / 1000) {
    console.error(
        'SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_ts` URL param should ' +
        'contain a hex string timestamp which points to the future.'
    );
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}
     
     /**
 * Returns query params from URL.
 * @return {!Object<string, string>}
 */
function getQueryParams() {
  const queryParams = {};
  location.search
  .substring(1)
  .split('&')
  .forEach(pair => {
    const parts = pair.split('=');
    queryParams[parts[0]] = parts[1];
  });
  return queryParams;
}

	stroyCleanUrl();
}

function lhsActiveStockWidgetToggle(btnval,id1,id2){
	document.getElementById(id1).classList.add('active');
	document.getElementById(id2).classList.remove('active');
	if(btnval == 'NSE'){
		for(var bseactiveindex = 0; bseactiveindex<bseactiveContentArr.length; bseactiveindex++){
			bseactiveContentArr[bseactiveindex].style.display = 'none';
		}
		for(var nseactiveindex = 0; nseactiveindex<nseactiveContentArr.length; nseactiveindex++){
			nseactiveContentArr[nseactiveindex].style.display = 'flex';
		}
	}else{
		for(var bseactiveindex = 0; bseactiveindex<bseactiveContentArr.length; bseactiveindex++){
			bseactiveContentArr[bseactiveindex].style.display = 'flex';
		}
		for(var nseactiveindex = 0; nseactiveindex<nseactiveContentArr.length; nseactiveindex++){
			nseactiveContentArr[nseactiveindex].style.display = 'none';
		}
	}
}
function lhsTopGainerLoserWidgetToggle(evt,activeIndex,selectedTab,id1,id2){
	var topGainerLoserArr = document.getElementsByClassName('lhsgainerloser');
	document.getElementById(id1).classList.add('active');
	document.getElementById(id2).classList.remove('active');
	if(activeIndex == ''){
		for(var lhsGainerLoserIndex = 0; lhsGainerLoserIndex < topGainerLoserArr.length; lhsGainerLoserIndex++){
			if(topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].classList.contains(lhsGainerLoserActiveExchangeToggle) && topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].classList.contains(selectedTab)){
				topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].style.display = 'flex';
			}else{
				topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].style.display = 'none';
			}
		}
		
	}else{
		lhsGainerLoserActiveExchangeToggle = activeIndex;
		for(var lhsGainerLoserIndex = 0; lhsGainerLoserIndex < topGainerLoserArr.length; lhsGainerLoserIndex++){
			if(topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].classList.contains(activeIndex) && topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].classList.contains('gainer')){
				topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].style.display = 'flex';
			}else{
				topGainerLoserArr[lhsGainerLoserIndex].style.display = 'none';
			}
		}
	}
}

<script>
var pixelPayloadObj;
var ipadress="";
function setIpAddress(v){
	ipadress = v;
}

function fireCapiService(eventName) {
    var capiXhrReqObj = new XMLHttpRequest();
    capiXhrReqObj.open("POST", "/datahash/capi/event/request", true);
    capiXhrReqObj.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/json");
    capiXhrReqObj.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
            console.log(this.status);
        }
    };
    var capiPayloadObj = {
        "token": getCookie('token'),
        "event_source_url": window.location.href,
        "event_time": new Date().getTime(),
        "event_name": eventName,
        "client_ip_address": ipadress
    };
    capiXhrReqObj.send(JSON.stringify(capiPayloadObj));
}

function callIpitoGetIP(){
	if((getCookie("token") && getCookie("_ht_clientid"))){
		try {
		    var ipifyUrl = 'https://api.ipify.org?format=json';
		    var ipifyXhr = new XMLHttpRequest;
		    ipifyXhr.responseType = "json";
		    ipifyXhr.open("GET", ipifyUrl, true);
		    ipifyXhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
		        if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
		            if (this.response.ip !== undefined) {
		                ipadress = this.response.ip;
		                setIpAddress(ipadress);
		            }
		        }
		    };
		    ipifyXhr.send();
		} catch (e) {}
	}
}
</script>

      function onPlayerStateChange(el) {
        
        if (el.data === 1) {
		 ga('send', 'event', 'video', 'video_play_clicked', 'video in story article', "");
        }
        if (el.data === 2) {
		 ga('send', 'event', 'video', 'video_exited', 'video in story article', "");
        }
        if (el.data === 0) {
		 ga('send', 'event', 'video', 'video_ended', 'video in story article', "");
        }
        
      }
      
var _player;

	  }
	 });

  function isOnScreen(element) {
	  var elementOffsetTop = element.offsetTop;
	  var elementHeight = element.offsetHeight;
	  var screenScrollTop = window.scrollY || window.scrollTop || document.getElementsByTagName("html")[0].scrollTop;
	  var screenHeight = window.innerHeight;
	  var scrollIsAboveElement = elementOffsetTop + (0.25*elementHeight) - screenScrollTop >= 0;
	  var adHeightToMinus = screen.width<=599 ? 100 : 300;
	  var elementIsVisibleOnScreen = ((screenScrollTop + (0.55*screenHeight) - elementOffsetTop - adHeightToMinus) >= 0);
	  return scrollIsAboveElement && elementIsVisibleOnScreen;
 }
 
function createVideo(){
	var youtubeScriptId = "youtube-api";
  	var youtubeScript = document.getElementById(youtubeScriptId);
	if (youtubeScript === null) {
	    var tag = document.createElement("script");
	    var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];

	    tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
	    tag.id = youtubeScriptId;
	    firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScript);
	}
}

function executeTPOnClick(subsStoryId) {
    count = count + 1;
    if (initPianoCalled !== true) {
        if (pianoScriptLoaded !== false) {
            tp.experience.init();
            initPianoCalled = true;
            try {
                pianoPaywallTimestamp["piano_executed"] = getTs();
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e);
            }
        } else {
            if (count < 10) {
                setTimeout(executeTPOnClick, 200);
            } else {
                console.log("Piano script load failed");
            }
        }
    } else {
        if (window.location.hostname.toString() == "staging.livemint.com" || window.location.hostname.toString() == "preprod.livemint.com" || window.location.hostname.toString() == "qa.livemint.com" || window.location.hostname.toString() == "stg-subs.livemint.com" || window.location.hostname.toString() == "pre-prod.livemint.com" || window.location.hostname.toString() == "staging12.livemint.com") {
            /*staging*/
            tp.push(['setAid', 'ZZEigyicsu']);
            tp.push(["setSandbox", true]);
        } else {
            /*prod*/
            tp.push(['setAid', 'Sgp5muRgpj']);
            tp.push(['setCxenseSiteId', '2480695787024000474']);
            tp.push(["setEndpoint", 'https://buy-ap.piano.io/api/v3']);
        };
        tp.push(["setUseTinypassAccounts", false]);
        try {
            var storyURL_piano = window.location.href;
            try {
                if (typeof document.getElementById('box_' + subsStoryId) != "undefined" && document.getElementById('box_' + subsStoryId).getAttribute('data-weburl')) {
                    storyURL_piano = domainURLEvents + document.getElementById('box_' + subsStoryId).getAttribute('data-weburl');
                }
            } catch (e) {}
            tp.push(['setPageURL', storyURL_piano]);
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e);
        }
        try {
            tp.experience.execute();
            try {
                pianoPaywallTimestamp["piano_executed"] = getTs();
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e);
        }
    }
}


function getUserRef() {
    var token = getCookie("token");
    if (getCookie("_ht_clientid") && token) {
        var userRefUrl = "https://accounts.hindustantimes.com/v2/piano/user";
        var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (xhr.readyState === 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
                userRef = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText).data;
                if (typeof userRef !== 'undefined' && userRef !== null && userRef !== "") {
                    tp.push(["setUserRef", userRef]);
                } else {
                    console.log('user ref not generated.');
                }
            }
        };
        xhr.open("GET", userRefUrl);
        xhr.setRequestHeader("Authorization", token);
        xhr.setRequestHeader("X-Client", 1003);
        xhr.send();
    } else {
        tp.push(["setUserRef", null]);
    }
}

window.addEventListener('load', function() {
    try {
        setTimeout(getUserRef, 1000)
    } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
    }
});
function setTpSection(storyId) {
    try {
        const targetBoxDivId = "box_" + storyId;
        const targetStorySection = document.getElementById(targetBoxDivId).closest("[data-vars-section]").getAttribute("data-vars-section");
        tp.push(["setContentSection", targetStorySection]);
    } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
        try {
            tp.push(["setContentSection", ""]);
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e);
        }
    }
}

function setTpAuthor(storyId) {
    try {
        const targetArticleDivId = "article_" + storyId;
        var authorName = "";
        const authEl = document.getElementById(targetArticleDivId).getElementsByClassName("author")[0];
        if (typeof authEl.innerText != 'undefined' && authEl.innerText != null) {
            authorName = authEl.innerText;
        } else {
            authorName = "";
        }
        if (authorName) {
            tp.push(["setContentAuthor", authorName]);
        } else {
            tp.push(["setContentAuthor", ""]);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
        try {
            tp.push(["setContentAuthor", ""]);
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e);
        }
    }
}

     function isGaa() {const params = getQueryParams(); if (!params.gaa_at) {return false; } if (!params.gaa_n) {console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_n` URL param is missing.'); return false; } if (!params.gaa_sig) {console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_sig` URL param is missing.'); return false; } if (!params.gaa_ts) {console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_ts` URL param is missing.'); return false; } if (parseInt(params.gaa_ts, 16) < Date.now() / 1000) {console.error('SwG Entitlements: The `gaa_ts` URL param should ' + 'contain a hex string timestamp which points to the future.'); return false; } return true; }
	/**
	 * Returns query params from URL.
	 * @return {!Object<string, string>}
	 */
	function getQueryParams() {const queryParams = {}; location.search .substring(1) .split('&') .forEach(pair => {const parts = pair.split('='); queryParams[parts[0]] = parts[1]; }); return queryParams; }

    function isElementXPercentInViewport(el, percentVisible) { let rect = el.getBoundingClientRect(), windowHeight = (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight); return !(Math.floor(100 - (((rect.top >= 0 ? 0 : rect.top) / +-rect.height) * 100)) < percentVisible || Math.floor(100 - ((rect.bottom - windowHeight) / rect.height) * 100) < percentVisible ) }

function formatDate(givenDate){
        var dateObj = new Date(givenDate);
var monthNames = [
  "Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun",
  "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"
];
var formattedDate = dateObj.getDate() + " " + monthNames[dateObj.getMonth()] + " " + dateObj.getFullYear();
return formattedDate;
}
